Local News

Northeast Customs Relocates Tax Collection

Finance Minister Song Issues Declaration and Speaks Yesterday

Unable to Collect Due to Rebel Seizure

Detailed Measures to be Announced Today

Central News Agency reports: Regarding the issue of blockading the Northeast customs, the 66th meeting of the Executive Yuan yesterday approved the relocation of tax collection. The detailed measures will be announced today by the Customs Commissioners of various customs. Finance Minister Song Ziwen summoned General Customs Commissioner Merleau and Jianghai Customs Supervisor Tang Haian at his residence in Shanghai yesterday morning and gave instructions on this issue. Minister Song also issued a declaration and a formal speech, which are specially recorded on the left:

▲Declaration The so-called "Foreign Minister of Manchuria" Xie Jieshi declared on September 15 that "Manchuria" will completely regard China as a foreign country in terms of customs, commerce, shipping, and even all other matters, and claimed that from September 25, all goods coming and going between China and "Manchuria" will begin to be levied import and export taxes. Therefore, the National Government instructed the Ministry of Finance that since the Chinese Customs is currently unable to collect legal customs duties at various ports in the three eastern provinces, it should close the Northeast customs for future orders. All customs duties to be levied should be temporarily levied at the customs south of the Great Wall to the extent possible. The detailed announcements are being issued separately by the Customs Commissioners of various ports.

▲Speech - The Japanese, under the guise of the "Manchurian authorities," began to seize the Northeast customs this spring, and in June, they forcibly occupied the Dalian customs. During this period, the National Government always expressed extreme tolerance and did not change the usual practice of transporting domestic products between the Northeast and other parts of China. At the same time, for foreign goods shipped from the three eastern provinces to other ports in China that had already been taxed, no additional taxes were levied. Because the three eastern provinces are Chinese territory, and 96% of its residents are Chinese people, if the government takes hostile actions against the Northeast, the result will only make the local Chinese residents suffer. Therefore, although the government was strongly urged by public opinion, it did not take any retaliatory measures, preferring to endure temporary tax revenue shortages rather than automatically starting to divide the three eastern provinces from other parts of China. In addition, the National Government, because the League of Nations Investigation Team was conducting an investigation, and at the same time, for the League of Nations' resolution to urge China and Japan to avoid any actions that would increase the severity of the situation, still paid attention to force under many provocative actions by Japan. This is also one of the reasons why the government had to take a tolerant policy. Now Japan, with the so-called "Foreign Minister of Manchuria" as its spokesperson, declares that it will disregard all international treaties, all international conventions, and all economic laws, and create a customs barrier between the three eastern provinces and other ports in China, so that the three eastern provinces will be isolated from other parts of China not only politically but also economically. This move by Japan is tantamount to forcing the 30 million Chinese people outside the customs to be permanently separated from their 370 million compatriots inside the customs. Not only that, but the so-called "Vice Foreign Minister of Manchuria" Japanese Ohashi Chuichi stated on September 16 that "Manchuria" will not allow inland opening except for the nationals of countries that recognize "Manchuria" and at the same time allow them to abandon consular jurisdiction, and will give them various benefits of residence, investment, or lease. Ohashi's remarks are tantamount to saying that the opening of the door to the three eastern provinces will change from opening to all powers and even to China itself to closing the door, and the only country that can enjoy the benefits of opening is Japan. However, although this kind of provocative behavior by Japan is unprecedented in history, the National Government will still not take retaliatory measures at present. What is being taken now is only a simple method to collect the customs duties that should have been collected at the Northeast customs at the customs outside the Northeast to the extent possible. Because China's interests in the three eastern provinces are far greater than Japan's interests in the three eastern provinces due to population and investment. If the government takes any action at this time to increase the difficulty of economic relations between the three eastern provinces and other parts of China, it would be something that the Japanese have been eagerly hoping for.

▲Measures - Yesterday, the General Customs Commissioner of Jianghai Customs in Shanghai received an order from the government to close the customs of Harbin, Niuzhuang, Andong, and Longjingcun on September 25, and recorded the measures for the import and export of goods to the above ports after the closure. (Our government, due to the Japanese occupation of our three eastern provinces, the National Government cannot temporarily collect legal customs duties at the ports of the three eastern provinces, and has ordered the customs of Harbin, Niuzhuang, Andong, and Longjingcun to be closed on September 25. All legal customs duties to be levied at the above-mentioned customs will be temporarily levied at other ports in the Republic of China. The tax collection measures for goods shipped to the above-mentioned ports in the three eastern provinces are as follows: (Domestic goods) (including factory-made goods) as before; (Foreign goods) those who have been given a license to exempt from re-levying and have stated that the import tax has been paid (as before), those who have always stated that the word "to be levied" should be paid at the port of shipment, and those who have always paid the transit goods at the port of arrival (pay the import tax at the port of transfer); (goods withdrawn from the customs warehouse,) pay the import tax at the port of shipment. The tax collection measures for goods shipped from the above-mentioned ports in the three eastern provinces are as follows: (Domestic goods) pay the transit tax and the transit tax surcharge; (Factory-made goods) the factory-made goods tax and surcharge usually levied at the ports of the three eastern provinces are all levied at the port of import; (Foreign goods) the import tax is levied. In the Dalian leased territory, because the Japanese authorities violated the agreement and refused to allow the Chinese Customs to exercise its functions in accordance with the Dalian Agreement, the customs cannot determine the source and destination of goods entering and leaving Dalian. Therefore, the tax collection measures are as follows: Goods shipped to Dalian, (Local goods) levy export tax (Factory goods) levy factory goods tax regardless of their final destination, (Foreign goods) the tax collection measures are the same as those for shipping to other ports in the three eastern provinces (see above). (Goods shipped from Dalian) All goods are subject to import tax, customs surcharges, and flood relief surcharges. All customs documents for goods shipped to the above-mentioned ports should be directly handed over to the shipper for collection. From September 25 of this year, all kinds of documents issued by the above-mentioned ports will be invalid. All transit foreign goods directly shipped from overseas to the ports of the three eastern provinces that do not leave the original ship in transit do not need to be taxed, or all transit domestic goods directly shipped from the ports of the three eastern provinces to overseas that do not leave the original ship in transit are also not taxed. From September 25 of this year, the tonnage certificates issued by the above-mentioned ports in the three eastern provinces will also be invalid.

German Aviator Arrives in Shanghai

▲From Japan to Shanghai in Four Hours and Twenty Minutes

▲Scheduled to Fly to Hong Kong Tomorrow Morning and Return to Europe

The famous German aviator Captain Wolfgang von Gronau arrived in Shanghai at 1:10 p.m. yesterday aboard the Dornier Wal flying boat. Captain Gronau took off from Kagoshima, Japan, at 8:50 a.m. yesterday morning (Shanghai time) and arrived in Shanghai in four hours and twenty minutes. He is scheduled to fly to Hong Kong tomorrow morning, then to Manila, and then return to his country via the Mediterranean Sea and Southern Europe.

▲Grand Arrival - Captain Gronau, accompanied by his assistant Captain Ziemeck, pilot Heck, and wireless operator Albert Lei, departed from the North Sea in Germany on July 22 aboard the Dornier Wal flying boat to make a round-the-world flight. After flying to the United States, he flew to the Far East along the route of Captain Lindbergh last year. After arriving in Kagoshima, Japan, he was delayed for two days, first due to repairing the aircraft and then due to bad weather. He finally flew to the Huangpu River near the Qingning Temple pier in Pudong yesterday afternoon and landed. Consul Fuchs of the German Consulate General in Shanghai, as well as German expatriates and aviation personnel, went to welcome him at Dinghai Bridge in Yangshupu. Captain Gronau flew the plane over Yangshupu at 1:00 p.m., circled twice, and then safely landed on the Huangpu River. The welcoming crowd waved their handkerchiefs and cheered. The Asia Company immediately released a small steamer to tow the plane to a nearby pontoon for mooring.

German Aviator Wolfgang von Gronau (Left) (Photo by Xu Tianzhang) Dornier Wal Aircraft (Photo by Xu Tianzhang)

At 4:00 p.m., Captain Gronau and others came ashore and stayed at the Li Cha Hotel and met with Chinese and foreign journalists. It is said that the mission of this trip is to prepare for the air route between Germany and the United States and to visit China and Japan. He is scheduled to fly to Hong Kong on Sunday morning.

▲Banquet Last Night - Consul-General Cronenberg of the German Consulate in Shanghai held a welcome reception at the Aviation Club on the roof of the HSBC Bank on the Bund last night to welcome Captain Gronau and his party of four, inviting Chinese and foreign dignitaries to accompany them. The guests included German Consul-General Cronenberg, Shanghai Mayor Wu Tiecheng, Eurasia Aviation Company

Manager Wang Zhiyuan, China Aviation Corporation General Manager Liu Peiquan, Aviation Club President Fores, and Chinese and foreign members, totaling more than 150 people. The guests and hosts enjoyed the banquet until 8:30 p.m. and then dispersed.

▲Carry Mail - Captain Gronau is scheduled to fly to Hong Kong and Manila tomorrow morning and carry mail. According to Shanghai Post Office news, a small number of letters and postcards to Hong Kong and Manila, if marked with the words "Flown by Captain Wolfgang von Gronau," will be accepted until 6:00 p.m. tonight.

Dockworkers Refused to Organize Yesterday

▲ Union Organizer Suddenly Attacked with a Blade

▲ Seven Arrested and Sent to Bureau for Interrogation

Dagong News reports: Since the Municipal Party Headquarters withdrew the former dockworker reorganization committee members and appointed new members to be responsible for reorganization, a small number of dockworkers deliberately obstructed the handover yesterday, resulting in a riot. The new organizers, Liu Defu and Xu Jianye, were attacked with axes and injured. They also created a disturbance at the Municipal Party Headquarters. The Public Security Bureau sent police to suppress the riot, resulting in the arrest of seven people. The details are as follows:

▲ Reason for Committee Removal: The former dockworkers' union reorganization committee was removed because the committee members were scattered and no one was in charge, resulting in the virtual suspension of union affairs. Disputes among workers arose from time to time. The Municipal Party Headquarters, in view of this, ordered a reorganization, withdrawing the old reorganization committee and appointing Liu Defu and eleven others as reorganization committee members to begin the reorganization.

▲ Handover Process: Since the Municipal Party Headquarters appointed new committee members to be responsible for the reorganization, the two sides agreed that the handover of documents and seals would take place at the Municipal Party Headquarters yesterday, the 23rd. Therefore, the committee members from both sides met in the conference room of the Municipal Party Headquarters at 2 p.m. yesterday to hand over the documents and seals. The former standing committee members of the dockworker reorganization committee, Shen Wenyuan and Wu Jiazhe, paid off all outstanding wages and expenses owed to the former members of the dockworker reorganization committee.

▲ Former Committee Members' Withdrawal: After the former reorganization committee members Shen Wenyuan, Wu Jiazhe, Gan Xinmin, and others handed over all documents and seals, they declared their willingness to withdraw from the dockworker reorganization committee and published a statement to clear their procedures. The statement is recorded as follows: (Shen Wenyuan's statement) To whom it may concern: I was previously appointed by the Municipal Party Headquarters as a standing committee member and general affairs officer of the Shanghai Dockworkers' Union Reorganization Committee. Due to the January 28th Incident, the monthly fees from Japanese-owned docks were suspended, resulting in a large accumulation of arrears in salaries for union staff and all expenses. Now, the Municipal Party Headquarters has ordered me to find a solution. I have recently raised funds from various docks and have paid off all staff and debtors in full on September 23rd at the Municipal Party Headquarters. At the same time, I have submitted a request to the Municipal Party Headquarters to resign from all positions. I will not be responsible for any matters related to the union after this. I am publishing this statement to clarify the situation. (Wu Jiazhe and others' statement) To whom it may concern: We were previously members of the dockworkers' union reorganization committee. The committee members have now been re-appointed by the Municipal Party Headquarters. All union affairs documents and assets of the former dockworkers' union committee have been handed over clearly on September 22nd. All accounts during our tenure have been cleared and are not related to the new committee members. Outstanding salaries for staff have also been paid off. We are withdrawing from the dockworker reorganization committee from the date of this announcement. We will not be responsible for any matters related to the union after this. Former standing committee member of the dockworker reorganization committee, Wu Jiazhe; reorganization committee members Gan Xinmin, Liu Defu, Huang Xianggu, Huang Zaoxiong, Zhang Sheng.

▲ Representatives Attacked: Yesterday, while the committee members from both sides were handing over documents and seals at the Municipal Party Headquarters, new committee members Liu Defu and Xu Jianye, accompanied by Municipal Party Headquarters supervisors Zhong Quan and Zhang Sheng, went to the former dockworker reorganization committee in Xiaojiuhua, Nanshi, to take over equipment. Unexpectedly, dozens of workers had been lying in wait inside the building. When they saw Liu and the others arrive, they closed the door and attacked Liu and the others with prepared iron rods and axes. Liu and Xu were immediately knocked to the ground, bleeding profusely. The representatives from the Municipal Party Headquarters were also slightly injured and rushed out of the door in a hurry. They reported to the Municipal Party Headquarters by telephone through the Social Affairs Bureau. The injured Liu Defu and Xu Jianye were ordered by the Xiaojiuhua police station of the first district and third precinct to be sent to Nanyang Hospital for treatment. It is reported that the two men suffered axe wounds to their heads and hands and were seriously injured.

▲ Petition Riot: After attacking the takeover representatives, the workers took four workers who were injured in the infighting during the attack to the Municipal Party Headquarters by car and held a collective petition. Unexpectedly, after arriving at the Municipal Party Headquarters, the workers closed the gate without asking for any explanation and rushed into the office, attacking anyone they saw. Zhong Quan, Li Weitai, Zhang Sheng, and other staff members of the department were injured. At that time, the gatekeeper stationed at the Municipal Party Headquarters, seeing the workers rioting, went to dissuade them. Unexpectedly, the leading workers Wu Mingfu, Zhou Hanqing, and others suddenly seized the pistol carried by the police officer. Because the police officer's strength was stronger, they failed to snatch it away. The workers then moved the trigger with their fingers, and two shots were fired immediately. Fortunately, the muzzle was pointing downwards, so no one was injured. In the midst of the chaos, Jin Tian, the director of the second district public security bureau, received the report and immediately led a large number of armed police officers to suppress the riot. At the same time, the police brigade of the Public Security Bureau also rushed to the scene upon hearing the news. Director Wen and the inspector also personally arrived at the scene to investigate and immediately announced a temporary curfew, prohibiting vehicles and pedestrians from passing through. Wu Mingfu, Zhou Hanqing, Wu Desun, Chen Baodi, Feng Binghong, Pu Linqing, Wang Guangcai, and seven others were arrested on the spot. The remaining workers fled in all directions. The suspects were sent to the second district office for detention. Traffic was restored at about 5 p.m. The four injured workers sent by the workers were sent to Shanghai Hospital for treatment by the Public Security Bureau.

▲ Municipal Headquarters Investigation: Afterwards, according to the person in charge of the Municipal Party Headquarters, the sudden refusal of the dockworkers to organize and the riot were actually instigated by someone. Therefore, the Municipal Party Headquarters advocated a thorough investigation and insisted on arresting the instigator for interrogation.

Women Workers at Silk Factories in Hongkou District Suddenly Went on Strike Yesterday

▲ Yuncheng, Yichang, Yuanfeng, Tongwei and Other Factories Vandalized

▲ Workers Surrounded the Union and Made Three Demands

▲ Union Held an Emergency Meeting and Refused to Accept

More than 5,000 women workers from twelve silk factories in Hongkou District, including Xiangcheng, went on strike one after another yesterday morning, causing disturbances and vandalizing factories. The situation was serious. The Public Security Bureau temporarily imposed a strict curfew, and the government authorities immediately sent personnel to investigate. The details are as follows:

▲ Cause of the Strike: At about 5 a.m. yesterday morning, when the silk factories were starting work, several people resembling female workers at the gates of Xiangcheng Factory on Tiantong Road, Yichang Factory on Wuzhou Road, and others, were propagating the demand for increased wages to the female workers going to work and preventing them from entering the factories. Therefore, only seven-tenths of the female workers at Xiangcheng Factory went to work. Most of the other female workers stood outside the factory gate and watched. The factory, seeing the situation was not good, immediately released the female workers in the factory and announced a shutdown.

▲ Vandalism: After Xiangcheng Factory released the female workers, the entire group of female workers flocked to Yuncheng Factory, dismantled the bamboo fences of the factory, and vandalized glass windows, cooked cocoons, and other items in the workshop. They then went to Yuanfeng, Renji, Tongwei, Yujing, Yichang, and other factories and vandalized them in the same way. Other factories, upon hearing the news, closed down one after another. Therefore, after 8 a.m. yesterday morning, all the women workers from twelve silk factories in the Hongkou area joined the strike.

▲ Police Arrested and Suppressed: After the women workers throughout the district went on strike, more and more female workers gathered in the Tiantong Road area. Li, the director of the fifth district and third precinct of the Public Security Bureau, upon hearing the news, personally led inspector Ren Huaipu and a large number of police officers to the scene to suppress the riot. However, the women workers were numerous and spoke in a disorderly manner, making it impossible to disperse them for a while. After the police officers persuaded them with kind words, fortunately, no unexpected incidents occurred. At the same time, the concession authorities also sent detectives to protect Tongwei, Yujing, Yichang, and other three factories.

▲ Factory Losses: Afterwards, the Dagong News reporter visited Yuncheng and other silk factories and saw that the bamboo fences at the back door of Yuncheng and the cooked cocoons and other items in the workshop had been vandalized. According to the person in charge of the factory, the estimated loss was more than 2 million. The iron gates and glass windows in the workshops of Yuanfeng and Renji factories were destroyed, with losses estimated at about 1,000 taels. The short wall at the gate of Yichang Factory was also demolished, and cooked cocoons and broken glass were scattered all over the workshop, with losses estimated at about 500 taels. Tongwei and Yujing were also vandalized, but the losses were relatively light. Other factories such as Yongji, Houfu, Weiyu, and others were not affected.

▲ Surrounded the Union: After the strike occurred, a large number of women workers, estimated at four or five hundred, gathered at the fourth district silk industry union, surrounded the union, and demanded that the union negotiate with the capitalists to increase wages and reduce working hours. Their attitude was very strong. Police officers, upon hearing the news, went to the union to maintain order. The union directors Le Shaorong and Dong Xingen repeatedly explained and persuaded the women workers. The women workers then proposed three conditions: (1) Wages of six jiao per day, (2) restoration of the weekly fee (i.e., Shen labor), (3) working hours not to exceed eleven hours. The directors agreed to submit the conditions to an emergency meeting for discussion and then negotiate with the factory. The women workers were satisfied and withdrew from the union. However, there were still hundreds of women workers scattered in the Tiantong Road area, waiting and watching until 11:30 a.m., when they gradually dispersed.

▲ Union Meeting: After the women workers proposed the conditions, the union immediately convened an emergency meeting. Those present included Le Xiaorong, Dong Xingen, Gu Xiaomei, Shen Xiufeng, and more than a dozen others. The meeting was chaired by Le Xiaorong, and the following resolutions were made: (1) The workers should be persuaded to resume work first. (Resolution) (A) Persuade the workers to resume work first, (B) inform the factory to resume work as usual tomorrow, (2) How should the workers' demands for the factory to reduce working hours and restore the original wage amount be handled? (Resolution) First restore personnel and then negotiate with the capitalists, and request the Municipal Party Headquarters and the Social Affairs Bureau to send personnel to mediate immediately, and appoint Le Xiaorong and Dong Xingen to personally request.

▲ Petition to the Party and Government: After the union meeting, Le Xiaorong, Dong Xingen, and six other representatives went to Zhang Peisi, the standing committee member of the silk factory guild, and presented their demands. Zhang declined, saying that the case was of great importance. The representatives returned to the union without success. Then, Le Xiaorong and Dong Xingen, two representatives, carried a petition and appealed to the party and government organs. The original petition is recorded as follows: A petition requesting immediate mediation. It is because the factory unilaterally increased working hours for no reason, which aroused the anger of all workers. Now, they have automatically held a strike and come to the union to demand that the factory negotiate, not increase working hours, and demand increased wages and restoration of the weekly fee (Shen labor). The union has negotiated with the factory without results. We specially appoint directors Le Xiaorong and Dong Xingen to humbly request that your association (bureau) immediately send personnel to mediate, so as to avoid the expansion of the labor unrest. It is truly convenient. Respectfully presented to the Municipal Party Headquarters and the Social Affairs Bureau.

▲ Capitalists' Meeting: After the labor unrest occurred, the silk factory guild convened an emergency meeting at 4 p.m. Those present included Zhang Peisi of Xiangcheng Factory, Huang Fulin of Yichang Factory, Wei Kunjiang of Yifengren Factory, Xu Bingyuan of Yongji Factory, Xu Chunqiao of Xinglun Factory, Zhu Liansheng of Houfu Weisi Factory, Wang Zhaxuan of Tongwei Yujing Factory, and more than a dozen others. The meeting was chaired by Shen Huachen. The meeting unanimously decided to refuse to accept the conditions proposed by the women workers. If the workers can understand everything, the factory will open immediately. Otherwise, they are willing to shut down. According to Shen Huachen, the chairman of the guild, to the Dagong News reporter, this labor unrest is very unfortunate and is quite pessimistic about the future of the silk factory. Since recent years, the silk factory's foreign trade has failed, and the economic bankruptcy is well known to all sectors of society. In the current state, it is difficult to maintain if you want to add more burdens. In my opinion, this labor unrest may not be due to the automatic action of the women workers, but rather that there are villains who are inciting it. Therefore, in this labor unrest, the factory will only wait for the fair resolution of the party and government. In short, if the factory is not burdened further, it will be able to open the factory immediately. Otherwise, it will only be able to close down.

▲ Authorities' Investigation: After the Social Affairs Bureau received the union's petition, it immediately sent Tan Peiyan to investigate the truth. The officer immediately rushed to both the union and the guild to investigate. Because the situation has expanded, there is no appropriate solution yet. It has been decided to conduct another investigation with the Municipal Party Headquarters today in order to handle the matter.

Large Quantities of Silver Dollars Being Transported

Since the Northeast was forcibly occupied by Japanese invaders, the Japanese have been secretly entrusting treacherous merchants to absorb silver dollars. In November and December of last year, nearly ten million silver dollars were transported from Shanghai to Dalian, Niuzhuang, and other places, which had an immediate impact on the market. After being discovered by the authorities, the customs was ordered to prohibit it. It has been absent for several months, but recently someone has been active again. Yesterday, a certain number of Tianjin-affiliated firms in this port received twenty-four boxes of silver dollars, and another number also had eight boxes of silver dollars, totaling 160,000 yuan, and handed it over to a British merchant ship to be transported to Da Yun Yichang and Tongli to collect. The huge sum of money was initially entrusted to Litai Chang and Yitaixing Customs Brokerage to declare the transport. The two customs brokerages refused to declare the transport because it violated the patriotic movement, so it was declared and loaded by Dong Shunji, and scheduled to be transported to Dalian this afternoon.

At this time of national survival, every citizen has a responsibility. Local News II

Arguments of the Three Lawyers in the Yun Huifang Case

▲ Chief Prosecutor Wang Zuzhe's Argument

The circumstances of the trial and verdict in the Yun Huifang case the day before yesterday were reported in yesterday's newspaper. Now, the arguments of the defendant's lawyers Zhao Chen, Shen Junru, Li Zuyu, etc., and the argument of Chief Prosecutor Wang Zuzhe are recorded below.

Lawyer Zhao spoke first, stating that the police accused the defendant of three crimes, but it is valuable to consider which of these the defendant should be responsible for and which the defendant should not be responsible for. The first crime alleged by the police is obstruction of freedom under Article 318 of the Criminal Code. The police lawyer argues that the sale of Japanese goods is an individual's freedom, which is permitted under Article 37 of the Provisional Constitution. However, that article also states (the state may prohibit those that harm the public interest by law). The so-called freedom must be within the scope of the law, so Article 17 of the Provisional Constitution stipulates that it should be protected by law as long as it does not harm the public interest; otherwise, it should not be protected by law. Since the September 18th and January 28th Incidents, the patriotic movements of our compatriots have been unanimously based on the national position, but unscrupulous merchants disregard everything and sell Japanese goods. This is the so-called action that harms the public interest. The law should not only not protect it, but it actually violates the crime of foreign aggression under Article 110 of the Criminal Code. The enemy's airplanes and artillery are still intimidating us every day, and the situation in Rehe and Tianjin is critical. Although war has not actually broken out, it seems close to war. After hearing this, Judge Qian instructed the lawyer to defend within the law. Zhao then continued, stating that selling Japanese goods is actually an illegal business. The government has repeatedly issued orders for long-term resistance. Dr. Sun Yat-sen's Principle of Nationalism clearly explains the meaning of resistance in the fifth lecture, stating that there are two methods of resistance: one is active and the other is passive. Passive means non-cooperation. Therefore, the boycott movement is in accordance with Dr. Sun Yat-sen's will and the government's orders. The unscrupulous merchants are undermining this movement and should be warned. They cannot be allowed to commit crimes themselves. Moreover, chambers of commerce and other organizations have long issued notices to boycott enemy goods. Even the League of Nations has provisions for economic sanctions. Without resisting first, how can we expect others to support us? Therefore, it is clear that the part of the accusation regarding obstruction of freedom is not valid.

The second crime is attempted murder under Article 282 of the Criminal Code. The subject of this case is actually wrong. The police believe that since the defendant committed the bombing in the French Concession, the bombing in the British Concession was also committed by the defendant. It should be known that the defendant has already confessed that the group was organized by two people. There are witnesses who have come to court to testify that the bombing of Yongchang Coal Store was not committed by Yun Huifang. How can he be held responsible for someone else's actions? The defendant's confession to the police was only a retelling of what Cai Yaozu said. This confession can only be used as a reference, and the evidence obtained through direct trial should be considered credible. Moreover, although the bombing of Yongchang injured someone, the injuries were minor. Why didn't the police prosecute him for the crime of injury, but insisted on accusing the defendant of murder? The defendant cannot be held responsible for this crime.

The third crime is possession of explosives under Article 200 of the Criminal Code. However, one bomb was found to belong to Cai. Although the defendant also had two bombs, they were all used up. The defendant cannot be responsible for this bomb either. In short, the first crime does not require punishment, the subject of the second crime is not the defendant, and the defendant should not be responsible for the third crime. According to the precedents of the Supreme Court over the years, the defendant is at most a continuous offender and should be acquitted according to the law. Lawyer Shen then argued that the crime of attempted murder alleged by the police is based on the defendant being a joint offender. However, according to the facts, the defendant did not conspire and the bombs did not belong to the defendant. Moreover, the defendant repeatedly confessed that he did not want to hurt anyone. Looking at the cases of the Cotton Cloth Guild and Maochang, his words are credible. When Cai threw the bomb, the defendant had not yet arrived at the scene, so he was clearly not a joint perpetrator. Therefore, the facts alleged are wrong. As for the bomb found, since it belonged to Cai, the defendant cannot be held responsible. What can be discussed is only the case of the Cotton Cloth Guild, but its purpose was to warn unscrupulous merchants. It was neither a personal infringement on an individual, nor a public infringement on an individual. It was as if it represented the public infringing on an individual. This situation is indeed special and should not be judged based on ordinary behavior. It is deeply in line with the provisions of Article 76 of the Criminal Code and should be given extra attention. Lawyer Li then argued that the obstruction of freedom is actually a continuous offense and should be acquitted. As for the attempted murder, the police also admitted that the bomb was thrown by Cai, but claimed that the defendant went with him. However, the defendant now denies it. The truth should be based on what was obtained through direct interrogation. Gu Cai had no intention of killing people, but because of the situation at the time, it was difficult to understand the things in the store, resulting in the error of injuring people. Lawyer Shen then supplemented his opinion, stating that the cause of the crime was not the defendant, but the unscrupulous merchants who sold Japanese goods. The police believe that in order to eliminate such incidents, the defendant must be severely punished. He is afraid that this will be counterproductive. The lawyers on both sides continued to debate the issue of continuous offenses for a long time before stopping.

Chief Prosecutor Wang Zuzhe then stood up and argued that the facts of the crime in this case are generally considered to be motivated by patriotism. However, violating the law is violating the law, and patriotic actions are patriotic actions. They cannot be mentioned in the same breath. Therefore, this case should be resolved based on the legal facts, without accommodating emotions. Looking at the three crimes alleged, in terms of obstructing freedom, the defendant has two actions, one in the French Concession and the other on Shanxi Road. Should these two actions be considered continuous and should they be considered as one crime? According to the Supreme Court's precedents, although the time and place are different, the intention is the same. It should be judged as a continuous offense according to Article 75 of the Criminal Code and should be acquitted. In terms of possession of explosives, these explosives were prepared for crimes such as obstructing freedom, so they should be punished as one crime. In terms of attempted murder, although the victim did not appear in court, the defendant cannot be accused of being present. However, according to the defendant's confession, he discussed it with Cai beforehand and went together at the time. He witnessed Cai throwing the bomb. Although he now claims in court that Cai went first and he went later, the suspicion of joint crime is difficult to deny. He should bear joint responsibility. Even if the defendant said he had no intention to kill, this is impossible to prove. However, the danger of the result of using explosives is foreseeable by everyone. Therefore, he should be punished under Article 294 of the Criminal Code and the term of imprisonment should be appropriately reduced according to Articles 30 and 77 of the same law.

Judge Qian then based his decision on Article 294 of the crime of injury and reduced the sentence by two-fifths within the applicable term of imprisonment and sentenced him to three months of imprisonment. Yun was released on bail by his original guarantor. It is still unknown whether he will appeal.

Wusong Yinxing Town Intercepts Two Kidnappers

▲ Four Bandits Suddenly Arrived at the Home of Xu Zhongtang

▲ Opened Fire Twice as a Warning, Robbing and Kidnapping First

▲ Police Arrived and Rescued the Hostage on the Spot

A major robbery and kidnapping case occurred yesterday at the home of Xu Zhongtang, a villager in Nanshao Lane, Yinxing Town, 7th District, Wusong Public Security Bureau. After the police received the news, they intercepted the hostage and captured two kidnappers. The details are recorded below:

Robbery at Xu Zhongtang's House: Xu Zhongtang, a 65-year-old villager in Nanshao Lane, three miles south of Yinxing, has two sons. The eldest son, Lansheng, is 17 years old, and the youngest son, Quansheng, is 5 years old. He has some farmland. Recently, 9 mu of his farmland was taken for use in the central urban area, and he received 200 yuan per mu for the land price, which aroused the coveting of bandits. Yesterday morning at around 9:00 AM, a car suddenly arrived with four bandits who spoke with a local accent. They held two pistols and arrived at the entrance of Xu's house, firing two shots as a warning first. They then rushed into the inner room and robbed 104 yuan in cash. Just as they were about to leave, they were still not satisfied. They happened to see Xu's eldest son, Lansheng, at the entrance,

So They Kidnapped Lansheng: When they were putting him in the car, the bandits only cared about the hostage. Xu Zhongtang took the opportunity to escape and rushed to the police station to report. Patrol Officer Tian Liang of the police station immediately led the police officers to the scene. They saw a car with the hostage still being watched by the bandits, sitting in the car. Patrol Officer Tian and others went forward to surround and arrest them. The bandits fled in different directions, and the police were able to

Rescue the Hostage on the Spot: When the police rescued the hostage, the car took the opportunity to drive away. At that time, the local defense team also came to help surround and capture the bandits. Patrol Officer Tian and others also tracked down the bandits. They found the four bandits eating at the home of kidnapper Ge Yousheng at No. 4 Xitangjia Bridge, 5th District, 5th Precinct. When they saw the police, they scattered and fled. Patrol Officer Tian and others went forward and

Arrested Kidnapper Lu Jiangsheng: One of them. A pistol was found on Lu's body. Unexpectedly, when the other three bandits escaped, they encountered Defense Platoon Leader Zhu Wenxiang and others who had arrived. Platoon Leader Zhu captured kidnapper Zhang Maofu. The other two bandits had already escaped. Patrol Officer Tian and others went to the home of the escaped kidnapper Shen Xinglin at No. 5 Zhoujiawan. Because Shen was not there, they arrested his wife, Shen Chen. A bullet casing was also found at Xu Zhongtang's house. The bandits Lu Jiangsheng and Zhang Maofu,

The Bandit Woman Shen Chen, etc.: And the bullet casing were all sent to the 1st Precinct of the 7th District of Wusong. After personally interrogating them, Director Yang learned that the bandits claimed that Lu Jiangsheng lived in Lujiagang, was 28 years old, and was invited by Ge Yousheng and Shen Xinglin to help them borrow money. The pistol was his. Zhang Maofu claimed that he lived in Zhangjiazha, 5th Precinct, 5th District, was 36 years old, and the rest of his statement was the same as Lu's. Shen Chen claimed that her husband invited Zhang Maofu and others to Xu Zhongtang's house to borrow money and did not rob them. Director Yang said that the hostage was rescued on the spot, and the evidence was conclusive. How could they be allowed to quibble? Moreover, it was found that Zhang and Lu were

Well-Known Local Thugs: Their usual behavior was terrible. Now that they have been arrested, they still dare not tell the truth. This is contempt for the law. If they are not severely punished according to the law, it will not be enough to warn the bandits. In addition to ordering the police to strictly pursue the escaped bandits, he also prepared a document to send the arrested bandits Lu Jiangsheng, Zhang Maofu, and Shen Chen to the Public Security Bureau for punishment according to the law. It is said that Xu Zhongtang's youngest son, Quansheng, was kidnapped by these bandits in August of last year. After asking someone to contact the bandits, he was redeemed. This is the second time that his eldest son has been kidnapped.

Niece Falsely Accuses Uncle of Kidnapping

▲ Holding a Grudge for Not Getting Money

▲ Many Receipts in the Handbag

At 10:00 PM the night before last, a woman dressed in a cheongsam and leather shoes, resembling a female student, accompanied by a man named Hu Yiping, went to the Third District of the Pudong Public Security Bureau to report that her husband, Xu Baolin, had been kidnapped by bandits and was being held in a house at No. 348 Yangjiazhai, demanding a large ransom, and requesting rescue. Director Zhang, believing that the case was of great importance, immediately ordered a patrol officer to lead the police to search the address. Unexpectedly, when they entered the house, the person whom Ms. Zhang pointed out as the kidnapper was not surprised or fled. Xu Baolin himself was also sitting in the house. The police took the man and Xu to the district, where Director Zhang immediately conducted a preliminary interrogation. Xu Zhang, 26 years old, from Zhejiang, residing at No. 24 Beller Road in the French Concession, stated that the defendant kidnapped her husband a few days ago and demanded a ransom, etc. Hu Yiping, 26 years old, from Anhui, stated that he saw her crying at the Nanjing Road Pier today. When he asked her why, she said that her husband had been kidnapped by bandits in Pudong and there was no way to rescue him. He felt sorry for her, so he asked the police for assistance. The police said that the matter was in the Chinese area and had nothing to do with them, so he accompanied her to the district. He did not know anything else.

The defendant, Tong Baorong, 44 years old, from Zhejiang, residing at No. 348 Yangjiazhai, stated that the plaintiff's accusation was completely false. He is the plaintiff's uncle. The plaintiff's son was sick and died a few days ago. Xu Baolin brought the dead child to his house. He had no choice but to take out three yuan to buy a small coffin to collect and bury the body. Because she had no money, she kept asking him for money. Because she did not get it, she held a grudge and falsely accused him of being a bandit. She also has an older brother named Zhang Zihua who runs the Baoshuntang Pharmacy at No. 108 Yangjiadu, etc.

The witness, Zhang Zufang, also reported that the plaintiff and defendant were uncle and niece. Director Zhang was greatly surprised by the confession. He immediately ordered Zhang Zihua to be summoned to the case. Zhang stated that the plaintiff and he were half-siblings. Their father passed away in 1926. The following year, his younger sister was introduced by a friend and married Wang Gongxia. Wang worked at the Capital Garrison Headquarters, and she went to Beijing with Wang. In 1928, she filed a complaint with the Nanjing Women's Association, accusing her husband of abuse and requesting relief. After mediation, they reconciled. Not long after, Wang went to Qingdao with Wu Siyu. She changed her mind and filed for divorce from Wang in the Suzhou court. At that time, she was having an affair with Xu Baolin, so she moved to Shanghai. Now, because her child had died, she wanted to move into his house. The neighbors advised her not to listen. After mediation by the neighbors, she was given some silver dollars to settle the matter. Unexpectedly, she fabricated the accusation that her uncle was a bandit, suspecting that she was mentally ill, etc.

Xu Baolin confessed that he had been having an affair with Zhang for many days and was not a legally married couple. Director Zhang, after hearing the confessions, realized that the case was clear. However, it was necessary to investigate why Ms. Zhang had used the trick of falsely reporting a kidnapping. He checked the handbag she was carrying and found many receipts. The content was roughly: After I met you, I have always loved you. We will grow old together. If I abandon you halfway, I will give you alimony, etc. There were also seven or eight notes saying, Please pay the bearer ○○ yuan in cash (one for 50 million, one for 100 million, and four or five for smaller amounts). Director Zhang asked Ms. Zhang about these receipts. She claimed that they were written by several of her former lovers. Director Zhang said that there were too many such slippery notes, indicating that she had been fooled by others several times. However, judging from her tone and demeanor, she did not seem to be mentally ill. Therefore, the case was very bizarre, but accusing her uncle of being a kidnapper without cause constituted the crime of false accusation. He ordered the witnesses in the case to be sent to the local court for questioning in the afternoon yesterday.

Preparatory Meeting of the Northeastern Refugee Relief Association

▲Nominating Members to Draft Organizational Plan

The Northeastern Refugee Relief Association was initiated by more than 40 leaders from all walks of life, including Wang Xiaolai, Shi Liangcai, and Du Yuesheng. Its purpose is to take into account national consciousness in addition to charitable undertakings. Yesterday at 2 p.m., the association convened its first preparatory meeting. Attendees included Mu Ouchu, Bei Songsun, Wang Yansong, Huang Renzhi, Yu Zuoting, Ye Jiaxing, Jiang Zhigang, Lu Wenshao, Chen Yizhou, Ma Jiliang, Yan Esheng, etc. Mu Ouchu was publicly elected as chairman. In addition to reporting on various letters, the meeting passed the association's green start. Luo Qinghua and Yan Esheng were appointed to draft all organizational drafts. Mu Ouchu also proposed implementation methods, which were slightly revised after Bei Songsun, Huang Renzhi, and others expressed their opinions. Finally, it was decided to convene a general assembly of all sectors of society on a scheduled basis after the draft organizational plan and specific methods are formulated to actively proceed.

Municipal Government Municipal Meeting

▲213th Meeting

The Shanghai Municipal Government held its 213th municipal meeting on September 16. Attendees included Yin Rugeng, Luo Panhui, Wu Xingya, Wen Hongen, Cai Zengji, Shen Yi, Jin Liren, Hu Hongji, Pan Gongzhan, and Huang Boqiao (replaced by Xu Yuanfang). Present as observers were Yu Hongjun and Chairman Wu Tiecheng, the Mayor. (A) Matters for report: (1) Chairman's report on the September 18th Memorial Day alert measures; (2) Report by the Director of the Public Works Bureau on the completion date of the Shanghai-Hangzhou Highway. The Xietu Road connecting to this road in the city urgently needs to be allocated funds for repairs to facilitate transportation. (B) Matters for discussion: (1) Reply to the original wording of Articles 5 and 6 of the Regulations of the Slaughterhouse Improvement Fund Management Committee. Resolution: passed. (2) Issue of payments for new municipal government and bureau construction projects. Resolution: The Finance Bureau will find ways to borrow 150,000 yuan for all construction payments for September and October. (3) Clearing of municipal public property. Resolution: Designated the Secretary-General and the Directors of the Finance Bureau, Land Bureau, and Public Works Bureau to discuss and handle the matter. The Secretary-General will convene the meeting. (4) Reorganizing municipal regulations. Resolution: Handed over to Councillors Yin and Luo for handling.

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Discovers Counterfeit Certificates of Domestic Goods

▲Letter to the Cotton Weaving Trade Association for Investigation

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce recently discovered that Guangxin Dyeing and Weaving Factory had privately manufactured the Chamber's certificate of domestic goods. A letter was sent to the Silk and Cotton Weaving Trade Association, asking for details of the certificate's origin for further investigation. The original letter stated: Respectfully, This Chamber has recently discovered a copy of the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce's certificate of domestic goods produced by Guangxin Dyeing and Weaving Factory. Upon checking the certificate stub of this Chamber, the factory has never issued a certificate from this Chamber. Based on the circumstances, it should be privately manufactured. Your association is requested to send personnel to inquire about the origin of the certificate in detail for further investigation. If the factory intends to deceive, this Chamber will send a circular to various places to detain the factory's products as a warning to those who intend to deceive. Furthermore, it is necessary to prevent similar incidents in other dyeing and weaving factories. Therefore, a separate list of the number of dyeing and weaving factory certificates already issued by this Chamber is attached for your association to check each factory to distinguish between truth and falsehood. This is of utmost importance. Sincerely, Shanghai Silk and Cotton Weaving Trade Association.

Labor Strike at Xiangsheng Iron Factory - Hefeng Went on Strike Yesterday in Support

▲The Dispute is Intensifying

▲The Labor Side's Attitude is Firm

Dagongshe reports that a major labor dispute occurred at the Xiangsheng Iron Factory due to the dismissal of workers. After three mediation attempts by party and government agencies, no agreement has been reached. The foreign manager of Xiangsheng insists on dismissing 106 workers before allowing the factory to reopen. After many days of stalemate, there is no solution, and the labor unrest is escalating. Workers at the Yangjingdong Hefeng Weaving Factory went on strike yesterday morning to support the reinstatement of the Xiangsheng workers and to prompt the capitalists to realize the situation. In addition to organizing a picket line to maintain order, the workers of both factories are extremely firm in their attitude and have resolved not to resume work until the capitalists agree to cancel the harsh conditions and not dismiss a single person. After the factory strike, the union has sent Director Zhang Linhua to report to the party and government agencies, requesting mediation. According to the labor side, if external forces intrude to disrupt the labor movement, they will seek a united response.

Postal Employees Will Have Delayed Promotions

▲The Union Issued a Warning Yesterday

According to a conversation with a committee member of the Postal Workers' Union, it was recently heard that a specialist member of the Postal Economic System Research Committee has suggested to the Directorate General of Posts to postpone the promotion schedule of employees in order to break the current difficult situation of the postal economy. The Directorate General of Posts also has plans to implement this. This move has caused considerable dissatisfaction among employees, because the current postal economic difficulties were caused by the separation of the Savings and Remittance Bureau. If the Savings and Remittance Bureau is not thoroughly recovered and this attempt to address the symptoms rather than the root cause is pursued, it will be difficult to break the current postal economic difficulties. A letter has been sent to warn them to abandon this plan to avoid public anger.

Jiangsu and Zhejiang Fisheries Bureau Emphasizes Fisheries Protection

Fan Zhilong, Director of the Jiangsu-Zhejiang Marine Fisheries Administration, is actively engaged in fisheries protection. With the fishing season approaching and patrols becoming tight, Fan Liangbo, captain of the Xinglong warship and concurrent inspector of the Jiangsu fishing area, has been specially appointed to inspect the patrol of the fleets in various areas to assess their performance.

Water Was Cut Off at Mingyuanfang Yesterday

▲There Is Also a Dispute at Fen'anfang

Guowenshe reports that the water company wants to force the installation of water meters, and citizens have been protesting in recent days. However, the company has successively cut off the water supply. Yesterday, the water supply was suddenly cut off at Mingyuanfang, Huade Road, causing panic among all the tenants in the neighborhood. In addition to severe negotiations with the company, members were specially dispatched to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Taxpaying Chinese Association, and other groups to appeal for relief. At the same time, the branch company also plans to cut off the water supply to Fen'anfang on East and West Huade Roads. The correspondence is recorded below:

▲Letter from the Taxpaying Chinese Association to the Shanghai Settlement Taxpaying Chinese Association: Respectfully, according to a letter from the mutual aid association of residents of Mingyuanfang, Huade Road in the settlement, a letter was recently received from the British-owned water company stating that the owner did not pay the water bill and decided to cut off the supply, and at 10:45 a.m. today, when the residents were preparing meals, the water gate was closed and the water supply was stopped. Water is one of the essential elements of life, and once it is cut off, the business lives of taxpayers in 184 buildings will suffer losses. For this reason, the members of our association, Zhou Yuantian and Zhang Shengyou, were dispatched to meet with your association to request assistance and to seek an interview. Immediately send a letter to the Municipal Council and immediately order the fire brigade to first open the public taps along the road for temporary relief to alleviate the immediate crisis. Notify the water company to open the water supply as soon as possible and handle it in accordance with the law. The association believes that such a situation can easily lead to serious consequences, and the Council is requested to quickly order the water company to open the water source and handle it in accordance with the law.

▲Fen'an Company Letter to the Officer of the British-Owned Shanghai Water Company: Regarding the letter sent on the 12th of this month regarding the water bill for Fen'anfang, Dongxi Huade Road, we have not received a reply regarding the reason for the exemption from rent and water bill based on the Municipal Council General Donation as the standard. Up to Friday of this week, our company sent personnel to your company to inquire about the above matters and explained the reasons. However, your staff insisted that the landlord was afraid of the tenants and waived the rent. Does this mean that the Municipal Council is also afraid of the tenants and exempts the municipal general donation for two months? It is necessary to cut off the water supply to blackmail the lives. The tenants are the ones who use the water, and the water bill should be collected directly from them by your company. There is no relationship with the landlord, and the payment of water bills by successive agents is an obligation, not a right. Our company has not received rent for February and March, but it is unreasonable to compensate your company for the water bill. Chinese and foreigners have the same feelings, and there is no such evil precedent in the world. Power is temporary, but reason is permanent. Please think twice. Please reply as soon as possible. If your company insists on using intimidation and oppression, then water is a necessity for life. For the sake of humanitarianism and caring for the lives of tenants, our company will store money and wait while protesting, and only pay the water bill first. Special letter.

▲Water Company Reply: Respectfully replying to your letter of the 16th of this month regarding the houses in Fen'anfang, Dongxi Huade Road, our company should still collect the water fee for the water supplied when the houses are still occupied. Your office must know this. If the tenant's rent has been resolved and rent is waived, or the Public Settlement Municipal Council temporarily waives the municipal donation, your office has no reason to request a uniform exemption from the water bill for two months. Furthermore, this matter has been investigated clearly by our company in March. The water bill calculated for the property is only calculated according to the number of occupied houses at that time. Based on this, it can be seen that our company has been extremely lenient. The payment deadline for the amount due by your office, which was explained to your representative the day before yesterday, will expire tomorrow. I am writing this letter specifically to remind you of this. If your office does not settle it, the supply will be stopped at that time. Special letter. To Fenxing Real Estate Company, British-Owned Shanghai Water Company, agent secretary, Luo Keqi.

Muslims Held a General Meeting Yesterday

▲Discussing How to Deal with Insulting Words in Nanhua

Local Muslims held a general meeting at the Nanshi Qingzhen North Temple at 5 p.m. yesterday. Mingshi Ha Shaofu was elected as the temporary chairman. First, Wang Yijun reported the discovery of insulting words (Why Don't Muslims Eat Pork?) in the 14th issue of the first volume of Nanhua Literary and Artistic Bimonthly and proposed methods of handling it. Next, Ma Tianying spoke, saying that the relationship between Muslims and Han Chinese in our country has been harmonious for a long time, and since the republic, the cooperation has been even closer. Moreover, there are 50 million Muslims in our country, and most of them are Han Chinese who believe in Islam. They are not uncivilized people. However, Shanghai, which claims to be the center of culture, has such extremely insulting words. There are many people in our religion who understand justice deeply. Even if they can temporarily suppress and wait for a legal solution, the company is willing to take the risk during this period of national crisis and wants to provoke the aversion between ethnic groups in the country. If it causes a civil war, the cause of the trouble starts with them. Although it is not appropriate to say that it is a crime of endangering the Republic of China, as evidenced by the fact that the British government in 1857 mistakenly added lard to the oil for wiping the guns of Indian soldiers, which caused a mutiny and a tragic bloodbath, because there are many Muslims in India who thought it was intended to insult them. From this example, it can be seen. After finishing his speech, Ha Decheng Ahun spoke, adding to the handling methods proposed by Wang Yijun: (1) The company should formally apologize to Muslims in the journal; (2) The Muslim General Assembly should write an article and order the company to publish it; (3) Ensure that there will be no more such defamatory words in the future; (4) The current issue of the journal should be burned publicly. The above methods were discussed and unanimously approved by the entire meeting. Then, the Muslim Association sent Ha Shaofu, Fu Jingzhi, and Wang Yisan to negotiate with the journal. It is heard that all four items have been fully accepted by the journal and will be published in the 15th issue.

Younger Sister Sues Her Brother to Award Her a Portion of the Inheritance

Wu Miaofu, the head of Chedaigjiao, Shanghai West, had five children during his lifetime. His estate was quite large. His son, Changsheng, was married, and his three daughters were married. However, his third daughter, Mituo, had not yet been married. After Miaofu's death, Changsheng inherited his father's legacy and frequently abused his younger sister. On New Year's Eve of the sixteenth year, he even drove Mituo away, causing her to work as a worker for many years to make a living. She repeatedly asked Changsheng to award her a portion of the inheritance, but Changsheng stubbornly refused. Mituo then hired lawyers Feng Xizui and Wu Zhengjiao to ask the First Special District Court to order Changsheng to award her a portion of the inheritance to support her life. Yesterday, Judge Yang Peng came to the Civil Court No. 10 for questioning. Mituo, dressed in rags and tears, accompanied lawyers Feng and Wu, as well as the defendant and the lawyers Zhang Zhengxue and Fang Jiahe hired by the defendant, all arrived at the court one after another. First, the plaintiff and defendant stated the facts, and then Judge Yang told Changsheng that no matter what the law is, the law is based on human feelings. The living conditions of you and your sister are very different today. If your sister is forced by hunger and cold and dies of starvation, how can a brother bear it? It is hoped that the lawyers on both sides will persuade the two parties to make every effort to reconcile in order to maintain friendship. Then, he adjourned the hearing to a later date and left.

Zhang Aweng, Impoverished and Ill, Cuts Off His Throat

▲Serious Injury and Life-Threatening

Zhang Aweng from Wuxi, 41 years old, lived at No. 30 Wenxingfang, Baikaier Road, Hongkou. He used to work at the Shenxin Yarn Factory. His wife, Shen, is 39 years old. Recently, Zhang has been ill for two months, and life has been difficult and economically distressed. After thinking about it over and over again, he wondered how to make a living. At about 8 p.m. last night, he suddenly had the thought of ending his life, so he grabbed a vegetable knife and cut off his throat, and his breath was dying. Later, his family sent him to Tongren Hospital for treatment by car. It is said that Zhang's injuries are serious and may be life-threatening.

A Truck Killed a Woman While Transporting Goods

Jin Zhao, a vegetable seller, went to the South Shanghai vegetable market yesterday morning to sell vegetables. Unexpectedly, a truck driven by Peng Fentai came and accidentally hit the woman, injuring her vital organs. The police officer on duty took Peng into custody at the Second District Police Station and sent the woman to Shanghai Hospital, but she died before she could be treated. Peng was sent to the local court for interrogation, and the head of the local neighborhood was ordered to report the autopsy to the local court.

Letter

To the Editor: According to our client, the Zhongfa Real Estate Trust Company, we have read a news item in your newspaper's local news section titled "Tenants of Laotianyu Alley Oppose Demolition and File Lawsuit," which is inconsistent with the facts. The demolition and construction of houses in Laotianyu Alley has been repeatedly notified to all tenants, and they have been asked to move out. The tenants have repeatedly requested extensions, and the deadline has long passed. Most of the tenants have already moved out, and only a small number of tenants remain, occupying the premises and refusing to move, which inevitably hinders the progress of our company's work. Our company has not received small rents of 500 yuan or 300 yuan from the tenants, nor has it stated that the leases can be extended for more than five years. If the tenants privately transfer the houses among themselves and there are transfer fees, it has nothing to do with our company. We should not use sensational language to harm our company's reputation. We are deeply concerned that false rumors will easily lead to misunderstandings. We have entrusted you to write a letter of correction. We hope you will investigate and promptly publish a correction in the letter column. Sincerely, Lawyer Xu Yannian, September 23rd.

Free Talk

Random Quotes from 93-Year-Old Ma Xiangbo About the World Fifty or Sixty Years Ago

Dr. Ling, on behalf of the Shen Bao newspaper, invited Elder Xiang to write a commemorative essay describing the academic atmosphere of the world over the past sixty years. After some discussion, I first searched for historical materials in the Xuhui Library and compiled a table of major events. After Elder Xiang read it, we had a brief chat.

In 1881 (the seventh year of the Guangxu Emperor), Elder Xiang recounted his interactions with Takezoe Shin'ichiro in Korea. That year, Korea was in turmoil, and China sent troops for more than a year, which brought a year of peace before the chaos resumed. Elder Xiang then went to the United States and recounted an event:

During the Guangxu eleventh year, the state of Philadelphia held a centennial celebration in memory of Washington. There were cadet corps, cavalry, etc., with the officers all being cadets. At that time, the French envoy to the United States, Gu, said to the elder: (Who dares to compete with this country!) (Quoting from the "Mirror to Reflect the People's Hearts"). Later, he traveled to England and visited famous universities such as Oxford and Cambridge. Elder Xiang said that many of the seats of famous people who had studied at these schools were still preserved as historical sites. He then went to Paris, where European universities still valued classical literature, with Latin and Greek being compulsory subjects.

He also recounted a historical event: When Italy was first unified, it seized the territory of the Roman Pope. When the army surrounded the city, the Pope, with benevolence in mind, ordered the volunteers from all directions who had come to defend the holy city not to fight. One volunteer, seeing through the world, entered a monastery and traveled across the ocean to China to preach. Elder Xiang even met him personally! This problem was only recently resolved. Italy still regards Catholicism as the state religion, which shows that governing with virtue is better than governing with force!

Speaking of Japan, Yang Shoujing took advantage of their disregard for Chinese studies to acquire a large number of ancient books and bring them back. However, although they disregarded Chinese studies, they still respected Chinese people. The world is very different now, and there is a sense of the vicissitudes of life in his words!

Guangzhou Miscellany

A Yan

|General Observations|

In the restaurants and teahouses of Guangzhou, the faces of the waiters are always expressionless. They do not call you "sir" or greet you warmly. Regardless of the status of the customers, they treat everyone the same. On the surface, they seem very indifferent, but they are very responsible in their duties.

Education is particularly developed. Ordinary families give their children a considerable education, so illiteracy is gradually decreasing. Almost all the people thronging the streets every morning, evening, and noon are male and female students. The female students wear white tops and black skirts, and the skirts are so high that almost their buttocks can be seen.

Women mostly mature early. At the age of thirteen or fourteen, their breasts are already high, so some people say that many girls over sixteen are not virgins. Their way of looking at men is somewhat different from Shanghai women. Shanghai women only look at you when you are not looking at them. When they meet a man they like, they often stare to their heart's content, making it impossible for the other person to cope.

The honesty of the rickshaw pullers is beyond our expectations. Bargaining will not exceed ten cents. They do not ask you to add money after reaching your destination. Even if you give them a coin to find change, they calculate according to the market price and never deduct one or two cents from you. This is enough to show the general nature of the staunch Cantonese people.

The concession in Guangzhou, Shamian, is separated from Guangzhou by only one river, but because the construction of Guangzhou city is very good, few citizens go to the concession. I personally did not go to the concession once during the half year I was there.

Every Thread is Hard-Earned

Juan

I recently accepted my friend Jiang Hongjiao's invitation to visit the Mei Ya Silk Weaving Factory. I was warmly received by Cai Shengbai and Gao Shiheng, the factory's general managers, who explained everything to me. I visited everything from the weaving factory to the printing and finishing factories. More than a thousand male and female workers were diligently working in an orderly manner, which is attributed to the application of scientific management methods. The printed crepe de chine and georgette produced are extremely soft and beautiful, surpassing imported products. However, the production process is very arduous. In the past, when people enjoyed a meal, they thought of the hard work of the farmers and sighed that every grain was hard-earned. Now, seeing the women weaving brocade on the loom, their ten fingers moving incessantly, I also sigh that every thread is hard-earned. I send a message to those who wear silk and satin: Remember this! Remember this!

Small is the Way to Go

Feng

|The Smaller the Better|

Nowadays, everything is about "small." Whenever a word is preceded by the adjective "small," the thing represented by that word becomes very popular. Here are a few examples.

The synonym for wife is "laopo." Adding the word "small" before "laopo" makes the wife more loved by her husband than without the word "small." The synonym for residence is "gongguan." Adding the word "small" before "gongguan" makes the residence more luxurious than a large "gongguan." "Xiansheng" is a synonym for prostitute. Adding the word "small" before "xiansheng" makes her even more marketable. A fair face is already pleasing. Adding the word "small" before "fair face" makes her even more lovable. Cigarettes used to be popular in large sizes, but now they have been scaled down, and small cigarettes are very popular. Mooncakes for the Mid-Autumn Festival used to be made as large as possible, but now they are made as small as possible and called "small mooncakes." The Austin car was originally very famous, but now fashionable people prefer to ride in a "Pei Pei" (i.e., "small") Austin. Even adding the word "small" to the synonym for vagrant, "dou luan," or to "bie san" seems to make them more popular than those without the "small" prefix. People get bored reading newspapers, so many "small" newspapers have sprung up to meet the demand.

Indeed, to be in the limelight these days, you need the word "small." You complain that society loves "small" in everything. Even in terms of countries, "small" ones benefit. Our eastern neighbor is shorter than us in terms of people, and smaller than us in terms of land, but this great country of ours is not as much in the limelight as our eastern neighbor. I wonder if shrinking the territory will also bring some of the benefits of the "small" prefix?

Lead Coins

Yan Chonglou

|A Kind of Social Pathology|

Perhaps the current society is a two-faced society of truth and falsehood! The already chaotic Chinese currency system, with its banknotes, silver dollars, large coins, small coins, etc., has now seen the emergence of lead coins. It is said that some unscrupulous people are casting silver coins with lead and passing them off as genuine, harming society.

In Shanghai, almost everyone has come into contact with these lead coins and suffered from their toxicity. However, lead coins are still being produced in increasing numbers and circulating freely. I have not heard of any measures taken by the authorities to crack down on them.

I once saw a rickshaw puller holding a lead coin, looking mournful. He said that he had run for many miles, and this strange coin was his reward. I think the tragedy caused by lead coins is not limited to the above-mentioned case.

A friend told me that he never has lead coins left in his purse because if he gets a lead coin that is rejected, he always spends it the second or third time. But I am not like that. If I unfortunately get a lead coin, I put it under house arrest. So I have accumulated quite a few of these coins.

It is said that some exchange shops specialize in buying these counterfeit coins at low prices and exchanging them for genuine coins to other people. These shop owners have obviously not thought about the crimes caused by using counterfeit coins. Otherwise, are they really heartless?

When receiving coins, people have to repeatedly check them. The person giving the coin is afraid of giving a lead coin, and the person receiving the coin is afraid of getting a lead coin. This is enough to reduce people's trust, let alone doing this on purpose to harm society!

I think this matter, though small, should also attract the attention of the financial authorities.

Shuobu Rotary Club

Silver Thread (23)

Jiang Hongjiao

(12)

Zhu Qilan wanted to give a speech herself, but since no one invited her, she went to her father and asked him to think of a way. Zhu Bofang was very willing for his daughter to be in the limelight in public, but since Director Yuan had already given a speech, the only thing left was to hold the unveiling ceremony. Moreover, it was getting late, the sky was gradually darkening, and they still had to take photos. It was impossible for anyone else to give a speech, so he just feigned asking: "Is there anyone else who wants to speak? Or is there any female guest who wants to speak?"

Zhu Qilan swallowed, cleared her throat, and was about to stand in the center of the stage to represent the female guests to give a speech when the county magistrate suddenly said, "It's getting late. Let's hold the unveiling ceremony, Mr. Zhu! Please tell the musicians to play!" Zhu Qilan, blushing, had to step back, hating the county magistrate very much, but there was nothing she could do.

The monument was built of Jinshan stone and was more than two zhang (about 20 feet) high. It was a simple triangular prism with a pagoda-like shape. The four large golden characters on the monument were "Zhi Zhen An Ning" (Stabilize the Town and Pacify the People), and a few lines of smaller characters read: "Yuan Tuantuan Kai, defended this land and resisted the enemy for a month, his hard work was meritorious, the residents of this town are grateful, and erected this monument to commemorate him forever. Municipal Committee Member Zhu Bofang, et al."

The base of the monument was filled with flowers and surrounded by the Party and National Flag, which was tied with two red ribbons. By simply pulling the slipknot of the long ribbon from afar, the flag could be detached and lowered.

The military music had already started. Zhu Qilan, full of spirit, held a large bouquet of flowers in her hand, first walked to the front of the stage and stood still, her face full of smiles. She pulled the ribbon, and the Party and National Flag slowly descended. There was a burst of applause from the stage and below. Who knew that the flag only fell halfway, as if it was caught on something.

The ribbon was broken, and the bouquet of flowers also fell to the ground. Zhu Qilan's face was flushed red. "Who did this?" The county magistrate was a little angry, and Zhu Bofang's face turned as white as paper. But Director Yuan looked at it and laughed because of it.

"Get a ladder and go up and take it down." Director Yuan said calmly.

The military band was out of luck and had to keep playing, blowing for more than ten minutes.

"The location of this monument is really not good. It is built against a large screen wall, and it is not surrounded by open space. And the screen wall is pitifully short, making it very difficult to match. If the two flags are removed, the form of the monument will be even more unsightly." The chief of the Public Security Bureau thought to himself, and thus noticed the screen wall.

"Hey! There's probably a ladder leaning against the back of the screen wall, isn't there? Isn't the top of a ladder showing on the screen wall?" the chief of the Public Security Bureau shouted.

Hearing this, Zhu Bofang, in order to redeem himself, personally went down the stage, ran to the back of the screen wall, carried the ladder out, leaned it against the screen wall, and personally climbed up to take down the flag. Who knew that there was a person squatting on the pagoda-shaped eaves of the monument.

"Ah! ... Ah! ... Yuan the Madman..." The scene was suddenly in chaos.
